<script type="text/javascript" defer="defer">

$( document ).ready(function() {
	$(window).load(function() {

		var theWindow    = $(window),
		$bg              = $("#bgFullWidth"),
		aspectRatio      = $bg.width() / $bg.height();

		function resizeBg() {

		if ( (theWindow.width() / theWindow.height()) &lt; aspectRatio ) {
		$bg
		.removeClass()
		.addClass('bgheight');
		} else {
		$bg
			.removeClass()
			.addClass('bgwidth');
		}

	}

	theWindow.resize(resizeBg).trigger("resize");
		$bg.fadeIn(1000);

	});
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
/*\
|*|
|*|  IE-specific polyfill which enables the passage of arbitrary arguments to the
|*|  callback functions of javascript timers (HTML5 standard syntax).
|*|
|*|  https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/DOM/window.setInterval
|*|
|*|  Syntax:
|*|  var timeoutID = window.setTimeout(func, delay, [param1, param2, ...]);
|*|  var timeoutID = window.setTimeout(code, delay);
|*|  var intervalID = window.setInterval(func, delay[, param1, param2, ...]);
|*|  var intervalID = window.setInterval(code, delay);
|*|
\*/

if (document.all &amp;&amp; !window.setTimeout.isPolyfill) {
  var __nativeST__ = window.setTimeout;
  window.setTimeout = function (vCallback, nDelay /*, argumentToPass1, argumentToPass2, etc. */) {
    var aArgs = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 2);
    return __nativeST__(vCallback instanceof Function ? function () {
      vCallback.apply(null, aArgs);
    } : vCallback, nDelay);
  };
  window.setTimeout.isPolyfill = true;
}

if (document.all &amp;&amp; !window.setInterval.isPolyfill) {
  var __nativeSI__ = window.setInterval;
  window.setInterval = function (vCallback, nDelay /*, argumentToPass1, argumentToPass2, etc. */) {
    var aArgs = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 2);
    return __nativeSI__(vCallback instanceof Function ? function () {
      vCallback.apply(null, aArgs);
    } : vCallback, nDelay);
  };
  window.setInterval.isPolyfill = true;
}

if (!Function.prototype.bind) {
    Function.prototype.bind = function (oThis) {
        if (typeof this !== 'function') {
            // closest thing possible to the ECMAScript 5
            // internal IsCallable function
            throw new TypeError('Function.prototype.bind - what is trying to be bound is not callable');
        }

        var aArgs = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 1),
            fToBind = this,
            fNOP = function () { },
            fBound = function () {
                return fToBind.apply(this instanceof fNOP
                       ? this
                       : oThis,
                       aArgs.concat(Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments)));
            };

        fNOP.prototype = this.prototype;
        fBound.prototype = new fNOP();

        return fBound;
    };
}

(function CAROUSELS() {

	var TOCarousel = function(container, interval) {
		this.container = container;
		this.interval = interval;
		this.items = null;
		this.itemsNo = 0;
		this.dots = null;
		this.current = null;
		this.next = null;
		this.currentDot = null;
		this.nextDot = null;
		this.timer = null
		this.interval = 2500;
		var self = this;
		console.log('Instantiated a container class for '+ this.container);
	};
	
	TOCarousel.prototype = {
		init: function() {
			var self = this;
			this.carousel = $('#'+this.container);
			this.items = $('#'+this.container + ' .carousel-itemLN');
			this.itemsNo = this.items.length;
			var dotsContainer = $(document.createElement('div')).addClass('carousel-dotsLN');
				for (i=0; i&lt;this.itemsNo; i++) {
					$(dotsContainer).append($(document.createElement('div')).addClass('carousel-dotLN'));
				}
			$(this.carousel).append($(dotsContainer));
			$('#'+this.container+' .carousel-dotLN').click(this.selectItem.bind(self));
			this.dots = $('#'+this.container+' .carousel-dotLN');
			this.current = this.items[0];
			this.currentDot = this.dots[0];
			$(this.current).addClass('selected');
			$(this.currentDot).addClass('selected');
			this.timer = window.setInterval(function(carousel){ carousel.loop(); }, this.interval, this);
		},
	
		loop: function() {
			this.next = $(this.current).next('.carousel-itemLN');
			this.nextDot = $(this.currentDot).next('.carousel-dotLN');
			if ($(this.next).length == 0) {
				this.next = this.items[0];
				this.nextDot = this.dots[0];
			}
			$(this.items).removeClass('selected');
			$(this.currentDot).removeClass('selected');
			$(this.next).addClass('selected');
			$(this.nextDot).addClass('selected');
			this.current = this.next;
			this.currentDot = this.nextDot;
		},
	
		selectItem: function(el){
			window.clearInterval(this.timer);
			var index = $(el.target).index();
			var currentBanner = $(this.items[index]);
			var dots = $(el.target).parent().find('.carousel-dotLN');
			
			$(this.items).removeClass('selected');
			$(dots).removeClass('selected');
			currentBanner.addClass('selected');
            $(el.target).addClass('selected');
			
			this.current = this.items[index];
			this.currentDot = this.dots[index];
			
			this.timer = window.setInterval(function(carousel){ carousel.loop(); }, this.interval, this);
		}
}
	
    window.TOCarousel = TOCarousel;

})();

</script>

<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
    
    function ShowPopup(popupURL, redirectionURL)
    {
        if(top.topNav == null) 
        {
            
                SB.base.deferWindowCommand(popupURL, 'popup', false);
            
            
            return false;
        }
        else
        {
            if (typeof(top.topNav.SB) == "undefined") { //Fix for free bets popup production issue 03/15/2013
                    top.topNav.SB = SB;
            }
            
            
                top.topNav.SB.base.deferWindowCommand(popupURL, 'popup', false);
            
            
            return false;                  
        }        
    }

    function ShowContactUsPopup()
    {
        if(top.topNav == null)
        {
            SB.base.OpenDivCheckLoginStatus('/t/forms/ContactUsNew.aspx','popBadSelect2','popVeil2','popLayer2',false);
        }
        else
        {
            if (typeof(top.topNav.SB) == "undefined") { //Fix for free bets popup production issue 03/15/2013
                    top.topNav.SB = SB;
            }
            top.topNav.SB.base.OpenDivCheckLoginStatus('/t/forms/ContactUsNew.aspx','popBadSelect2','popVeil2','popLayer2',false);
        }
    }

</script>
